 With this, the police is now trying to reach the attackers by checking this CCTV footage
 police kii ore se jari do tasveeron main teen log bike par jate dikh rahe hai jinhone apane chehre dhake hue hai
 In the past, there have been fatal attacks on Bukhari, even before the death of Bukhari, there have been many fatal attacks
 july 1996 main aatankiyon ne unhen saat ghante tak anantnag main bandhak banaakar rakhaa tha
 In 2000, Bukhari was given police protection after being threatened with death
 saal 2006 main bhi bukhari par jaanaleva hamalaa kiya gaya tha
 a year ago he received threats from Pakistani terrorists
 iske baad unhen eks shrenee kii suraksha mili thi, jisamen unke saath do surakshakarmi tainaat rahete the
 Shujaat Bukhari continued to step by step with the government continuously to resolve indo-pak peace talks and Kashmir dispute
 iske saath hi unke akhbaar rising kashmir ko ghati kii aawaaj kaha jaataa he
 Despite the threat of life, he always used to say that his pen cannot be pacified by showing fear of gun
 sarkaar kii nijeekaran kii niti ke virodh main desh bhar ke saarvajanikshetra ke bank karmchaariyon kii do din kii hadtaal buudhvaar ko shuru ho gai
 Bankers were scheduled to go on strike after talks between Chief Labor Commissioner SK Mukhopadhyay and United Forum of Bank Union (UFBU) leaders failed on Tuesday
 tamilnadu main kareeb 60,000 bank karmchaaree hadtaal main shaamil hai
 CHF Venkatachalam, convenor of UFBU here, said that branches of state-run banks along with some private banks will remain closed due to the strike and we will also take out a procession in Chennai today
 kerala main bhi bank band hai or rajyabar main karmchaaree bainkon ke saamne pradarshan kar rahe hai
 Businessmen say they will face a lot of difficulty due to the banks being closed for two days
 gauratlab he ki bainkon ke vibhinn union banking kshetra main pratyaksh videshi nivesh (epadiai) kaa virodh karte aa rahe hai

 ayodhya maamle ko lekar supreme court ke faisle par samiksha ke liye yojit jamiyat ulema hind rashtriya kaarysmiti baithak ke nishkarsh main adhyaksh moulana arshad madani ne kaha he ki court kaa faisla samaj se pare he
 In the eyes of law and justice, there was and is a Babri Masjid and till the doom, the mosque will remain, irrespective of its name or appearance
 madani ne kaha ki court ke faisle se ek baat spasht he ki masjid kaa nirmaan kisi mandir ko todakar nahin kiya gaya or naa hi kisi mandir kii jagah par hua
 This stain on the issue of Muslims was washed away due to this court, in which there were allegations of breaking the temple or building a mosque on the site of the temple
 punarvichaar yachika par charchaa karte hue madani ne kaha ki jamiyat ne ek panel banaaya he jo vakeelon or shikshavidon se tathyon or pramaanon ke aadhaar par nishkarsh nikaalega kii punarvichaar yachika daakhil karnaa he yaa nahin
 Madani said about the court's decision that in a way the court believed that it was wrong to keep the idol inside the mosque and then break it, yet the court gave the land to the people who kept the idol in the mosque and then broke the mosque
 court dwaara 5 acre jameen mudde par madani ne kaha ki musalmaan kabhi bhi jameen kaa mohataaj nahin rahaa or ye jameen court ne sunni vakf board ko di he or meri salaah ye he ki board ko jameen nahin sweekaar kerani chahie
 In response to a question, Madani said that it is meaningless to take the Babri Masjid issue to the International Court, the court is ours, the country is ours and we respect the decision of the Supreme Court
 ham jo kaarywahi karenge desh ke samvidhan or kanoon ke anusaar karenge
 In the end Madani said that if the mosque had not been demolished, would the court have said that the temple should be built by breaking the mosque? We are satisfied that the court admitted that the mosque was not built by demolishing the temple, but regrettably, contrary to the evidence and facts, the court gave the entire land to Ram Lala
 madani ne kaha ki jab court ne masjid vidhwans ko avaidh kaha or ise kanoon kaa ulanghan mana to phir is aparaadh main shaamil aparaadhiyon par rojaanaa sunwaayee honi chahie
 Union Finance Minister Arun Jaitley said on Friday that the Finance Ministers of all states are in favor of implementing the Goods and Services Tax (GST) soon
 rajyon ke vittamantriyon ke saath bajet purv baithak ke baad jetali ne kaha ki sabhi rajya jiesti ko shighrata se lagu karne ke paksh main hai
 The government plans to implement GST from April 1, 2016
 pichley saptaah sarkaar ne loksabhaa main jiesti vidheyak pesh kiya tha
 According to the government, this is the single most important tax reform since 1947
 is vidheyak ke nirbaadh karyanvan ke liye jetali pehle hi sansad ko bataa chuke hai ki teen saal ke bheetar centre sarkaar rajyon kii 34,000 karod rupee kii bakaayaa muaavja raashi kaa bhugtan kar degaa
 In a meeting held on Friday, Jaitley also said that some states want to increase the limit of Fiscal Responsibility and Budget Management Act 2003 (FRBMA) so that states can borrow more
 etharabime adhinium ko sansad ne paarit kiya tha
 The objective was to institutionalize financial discipline, reduce fiscal deficit and improve macroeconomic management
